event = {

		}

event = {
	id = 1400000022  
	random = no
	country = CHI
	save_date = yes
	
		trigger = {
	OR = {
		AND = { NOT = { exists = CHC } event = { id = 1400000014 days = 100 } }		
		AND = { event = { id = 1400000015 days = 100 } }
		AND = { event = { id = 1400000023 days = 100 } }
		}
		flag = CHI_institutional_politics
		NOT = { ispuppet = yes }
		NOT = { flag = KMT_Instability }
		NOT = { flag = CHI_internal_dissent }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1928 }
    offset = 10
    deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	style = 2
	picture = "China_National Assembly"
	name = "National Assembly election"
	desc = "EVT_1400000022_desc"
	action = {
		name = "the road to Institutional Democratization" #They are also not democratic.  in OTL, it became democratized after 1991-1992, but it was also limited to Taiwan.
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 6 } 
		command = { type = set_domestic which = political_left value = 4 }
		command = { type = set_domestic which = freedom value = 6 }
		command = { trigger = { minister = 55001 } type = headofstate which = 55001 } #Chiang Kai-shek
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { minister = 55001 } } type = headofstate which = 55350 } #Sun fo, #Chiang Kai-shek assassinated by the opposition

event = {
	id = 1400001008
	random = no
	country = U63 
	name = "Discussion of Anti-Chiang coalition"
	desc = ""
	style = 2
	picture = "ccip_gmd"
	save_date = yes

	trigger = {	
		exists = CHI
		NOT = { war = { country = CHI country = CGX } }
		NOT = { war = { country = CHI country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = JAP country = CGX } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = CGX } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = CGX } }
		OR = { #either Guangxi is not a puppet, or it is a puppet of CHI
			NOT = { ispuppet = CGX }
			puppet = { country = CGX country = CHI }
			NOT = { ispuppet = U63  }
			puppet = { country = U63  country = CHI }
		}
		OR = { #either CHI is not a puppet, or it controls CGX as a puppet anyway
			NOT = { ispuppet = CHI }
			puppet = { country = U63  country = CHI }
			NOT = { ispuppet = CHI }
			puppet = { country = CGX country = CHI }
		}
	}

    date = { day = 29 month = may year = 1936 }
    offset = 30
    deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

 event = {
     id = 1400007501
     random = no
     country = JAP
	 save_date = yes
     style = 2

   decision = {
     NOT = { flag = JAP_ECO_MANCHURIA }
     OR = {
       AND = {
         OR = {
              alliance = { country = MAN country = JAP }
              puppet = { country = MAN country = JAP }
         }
         owned = { province = 1199 data = MAN }
         control = { province = 1199 data = MAN }
         owned = { province = 1214 data = MAN }
         control = { province = 1214 data = MAN }
       }

       AND = {
         owned = { province = 1199 data = JAP }
         control = { province = 1199 data = JAP }
         owned = { province = 1214 data = JAP }
         control = { province = 1214 data = JAP }
       }
     }
   }
	decision_trigger = {
	     NOT = { flag = JAP_ECO_MANCHURIA }
     OR = {
       AND = {
         OR = {
              alliance = { country = MAN country = JAP }

				control = { province = 160 data = -1 }

	}

	id = 1400010023
	random = no
	country = USA

	decision = {
			OR = {
			alliance = { country = USA country = ENG }
			alliance = { country = USA country = CAN }
			}

			war = { country = GER country = ENG }
			war = { country = GER country = CAN }
			}
			NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = ENG } }
			NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = USA } }
	}
			
	decision_trigger = { 
			OR = {
			alliance = { country = USA country = ENG }
			alliance = { country = USA country = CAN }
			}
			NOT = { alliance_leader = { country = USA } }
			NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = ENG } }
			NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = USA } }
	}
	
	trigger = {
			NOT = { alliance_leader = { country = USA } }
			OR = {
			alliance = { country = USA country = ENG }
			alliance = { country = USA country = CAN }
			}

			war = { country = GER country = ENG }
			war = { country = GER country = CAN }
			}

			NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = USA } }
	}
